BRA_setup_UDN_aligned = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 2 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 7 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 12 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 6 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 10 }
}

BRA_setup_PTB_aligned = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 13 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 3 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 9 }
}

BRA_setup_PSD_aligned = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 11 }
}

BRA_setup_PSP_aligned = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 8 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 4 }
}

BRA_setup_low_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 5 }
}
BRA_setup_med_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 10 }
}
BRA_setup_high_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 20 }
}

BRA_setup_neg_low_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -5 }
}
BRA_setup_neg_med_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -10 }
}
BRA_setup_neg_high_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -20 }
}



BRA_modify_electoral_chances_nationwide = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 22
		value = i

		add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = i }
	}
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}
BRA_modify_electoral_chances_amazonia = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 2 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 11 }
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}
BRA_modify_electoral_chances_central_west = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 6 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 9 }
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}

	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 13 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 18 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 19 }
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes

	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 5 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 7 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 10 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 16 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 20 }

BRA_modify_electoral_chances_northeast = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 3 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 4 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 8 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 12 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 14 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 15 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 17 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 21 }
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}
BRA_modify_electoral_chances = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
		value = i
		index = k
		break = bo

		set_temp_variable = { lo = i }
		set_temp_variable = { hi = i }
		add_to_temp_variable = { hi = 1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { lo = 8 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { hi = 8 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = lo
			end = hi
			value = j
			break = bi

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { BRA_candidate_identities^j = 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties value = BRA_candidate_parties^j } }
				add_to_variable = { BRA_candidate_popularities^j = BRA_modify_amnt }
			}
		}
	}

	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	BRA_update_leading_parties = yes
	BRA_senate_update_selected_state = yes
}
